    		rootFolder

    Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

    		maxFileSize

    Rollover threshold in bytes; a write that would exceed it opens a new file (SRS-LMBR-033).

    		maxFileCount

    Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

    		baseName

    Leading name applied to each file for sorting. Cannot contain an underscore, which is reserved as the timestamp separator in generated file names.

    		extension

    File extension without the dot (e.g. "csv").

    		delimiter

    Column separator passed to the CSVLayout (e.g. "," or a tab).

    		calendarFolderTree

    When TRUE, place files in a dated sub-folder hierarchy under the root (SRS-LMBR-036).

FilterDTOin

String DTO mirror of Filter, used only as the Unflatten From JSON target and merge currency (SDD 4.2). mode is a FilterMode member name; levelMin/levelMax are Severity member names; tagPrefix is unchanged. Resolve maps this to the native Filter (names to enums). Not part of the public API.

    		mode

    Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

    accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

    Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

    threshold.

    Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

    range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

    		levelMin

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		levelMax

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

Lumberjack.lvlib:ValidateLumberjackConfigDTO.vi

Pure DTO validation. Fail-fast checks on a merged LumberjackConfigDTO, returning a descriptive error on the first invalid field: schema version, enum-name membership, file size, and filename safety of baseName and extension (SRS-LMBR-048, codes 5020-5039). Passes the DTO through on success. No I/O.

Merged DTO -> descriptive error on first invalid field (else passthrough).

 BaselineDTO

Top-level string DTO mirror of LumberjackConfig and the Unflatten From JSON target for the whole config file (SDD 4.2). globalThreshold is a Severity member name; defaultFileAppender is a FileAppenderConfigDTO; schemaVersion is unchanged. Merge overlays JSON onto a baseline of this type; Resolve maps the validated result to the native LumberjackConfig.

    		schemaVersion

    JSON schema version; lets the validator reject configs it doesn't understand (SDD §4.2).

    		globalThreshold

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		defaultFileAppender

    Configuration for a file appender: an AppenderConfig nested as `common` plus file-specific fields. Field names match the JSON keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly (SRS-LMBR-030, 032-040). `delimiter` is fed into the CSVLayout the appender builds, not a separate setting (SDD 5.4).

      		common

      Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig). Carries identity, the per-appender authoritative threshold and selection filter (stage-2), backpressure settings, and the layout strategy. Field names match the JSON `common` keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly; `layout` is a Layout object set in code, not via JSON.

        		id

        Unique appender id, matching the appender's common config id.

        		threshold

        String representation of severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

        offset math required).

        Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

        DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

        Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

        is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

        		filter

        Per-appender selection filter, applied after the appender threshold (SRS-LMBR-026, 027). In mirror mode, accept every statement at or above the appender threshold. In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

          		mode

          Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

          accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

          Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

          threshold.

          Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

          range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

          		levelMin

          Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

          Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

          Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

          		levelMax

          Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

          Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

          Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

          		tagPrefix

          Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

        		queueBound

        Maximum intake queue depth; 0 means unbounded (SRS-LMBR-055, 056).

        		dropPolicy

        Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

        full. Applies only when the appender's queue bound is greater than 0;

        new one. Favors recency.

        DropNewest: reject the incoming statement, keep what is already queued.

        LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

        statements first.

        		useUTC

        When TRUE, timestamps are formatted in UTC; when FALSE, in the local time zone. Per-appender and stamped onto the layout at Init, so different appenders may use different time frames (SRS-LMBR-013).

      		fileConfig

      Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

        		rootFolder

        Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

        		maxFileSize

In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

      		mode

      Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

      accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

      Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

      threshold.

      Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

      range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

      		levelMin

      Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

      thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

      statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

      offset math required).

      Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

      DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

      Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

      is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

      		levelMax

      Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

      thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

      statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

      offset math required).

      Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

      DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

      Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

      is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

      		tagPrefix

      Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

    		queueBound

    Maximum intake queue depth; 0 means unbounded (SRS-LMBR-055, 056).

    		dropPolicy

    Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

    full. Applies only when the appender's queue bound is greater than 0;

    an unbounded queue never drops. Discards are surfaced as a synthetic

    "N statements dropped" record, so loss is observable.

    DropOldest (default): discard the oldest queued statement to admit the

    new one. Favors recency.

    DropNewest: reject the incoming statement, keep what is already queued.

    LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

    statements first.

    		useUTC

    When TRUE, timestamps are formatted in UTC; when FALSE, in the local time zone. Per-appender and stamped onto the layout at Init, so different appenders may use different time frames (SRS-LMBR-013).

error in (no error)

error in can accept error information wired from VIs previously called. Use this information to decide if any functionality should be bypassed in the event of errors from other VIs.

Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		status

    status is TRUE (X) if an error occurred or FALSE (checkmark) to indicate a warning or that no error occurred.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		code

    code is the error or warning code.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		source

    source describes the origin of the error or warning.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

AppenderConfig

Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig). Carries identity, the per-appender authoritative threshold and selection filter (stage-2), backpressure settings, and the layout strategy. Field names match the JSON `common` keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly; `layout` is a Layout object set in code, not via JSON.

FileAppenderConfig

Configuration for a file appender: an AppenderConfig nested as `common` plus file-specific fields. Field names match the JSON keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly (SRS-LMBR-030, 032-040). `delimiter` is fed into the CSVLayout the appender builds, not a separate setting (SDD 5.4).

    		common

    Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig).     		file

    Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

      		rootFolder

      Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

      		maxFileSize

      Rollover threshold in bytes; a write that would exceed it opens a new file (SRS-LMBR-033).

      		maxFileCount

      Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

      		baseName

      Leading name applied to each file for sorting. Cannot contain an underscore, which is reserved as the timestamp separator in generated file names.

      		extension

      File extension without the dot (e.g. "csv").

      		delimiter

      Column separator passed to the CSVLayout (e.g. "," or a tab).

      		calendarFolderTree

      When TRUE, place files in a dated sub-folder hierarchy under the root (SRS-LMBR-036).

Lumberjack.lvlib:FileAppenderConfigFromDTO.vi

 error in (no error)

error in can accept error information wired from VIs previously called. Use this information to decide if any functionality should be bypassed in the event of errors from other VIs.

Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		status

    status is TRUE (X) if an error occurred or FALSE (checkmark) to indicate a warning or that no error occurred.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		code

    code is the error or warning code.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		source

    source describes the origin of the error or warning.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

FileAppenderConfigDTO

String DTO mirror of FileAppenderConfig (SDD 4.2). common is an AppenderConfigDTO; rootFolder is a string (Resolve converts to Path); baseName/maxFileSize/maxFileCount/extension/delimiter/calendarFolderTree/useUTC are unchanged. Resolve maps this to the native FileAppenderConfig.

    		common

    Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig). Carries identity, the per-appender authoritative threshold and selection filter (stage-2), backpressure settings, and the layout strategy. Field names match the JSON `common` keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly; `layout` is a Layout object set in code, not via JSON.

      		id

      Unique appender id, matching the appender's common config id.

      		threshold

      String representation of severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

      offset math required).

      Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

      DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

      Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

      is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

      		filter

      Per-appender selection filter, applied after the appender threshold (SRS-LMBR-026, 027). In mirror mode, accept every statement at or above the appender threshold. In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

        		mode

        Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

        accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

        Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

        threshold.

        Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

        range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

        		levelMin

        Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

        Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

        Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

        		levelMax

        Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

        Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

        Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

        		tagPrefix

        Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

      		queueBound

      Maximum intake queue depth; 0 means unbounded (SRS-LMBR-055, 056).

      		dropPolicy

      Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

      full. Applies only when the appender's queue bound is greater than 0;

      an unbounded queue never drops. Discards are surfaced as a synthetic

      "N statements dropped" record, so loss is observable.

      DropOldest (default): discard the oldest queued statement to admit the

      new one. Favors recency.

      DropNewest: reject the incoming statement, keep what is already queued.

      LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

      statements first.

      		useUTC

      When TRUE, timestamps are formatted in UTC; when FALSE, in the local time zone. Per-appender and stamped onto the layout at Init, so different appenders may use different time frames (SRS-LMBR-013).

    		fileConfig

    Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

      		rootFolder

      Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

      		maxFileSize

      Rollover threshold in bytes; a write that would exceed it opens a new file (SRS-LMBR-033).

      		maxFileCount

      Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

      		baseName

      Leading name applied to each file for sorting. Cannot contain an underscore, which is reserved as the timestamp separator in generated file names.

      		extension

      File extension without the dot (e.g. "csv").

      		delimiter

      Column separator passed to the CSVLayout (e.g. "," or a tab).

      		calendarFolderTree

      When TRUE, place files in a dated sub-folder hierarchy under the root (SRS-LMBR-036).

Lumberjack.lvlib:FilterDTOFromNative.vi

 Filter

Per-appender selection filter, applied after the appender threshold (SRS-LMBR-026, 027). In mirror mode, accept every statement at or above the appender threshold. In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

    		mode

    Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

    accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

    Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

    threshold.

    Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

    range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

    		levelMin

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		levelMax

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		tagPrefix

    Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

Filter

Per-appender selection filter, applied after the appender threshold (SRS-LMBR-026, 027). In mirror mode, accept every statement at or above the appender threshold. In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

    		mode

    Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

    accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

    Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

    threshold.

    Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

    range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

    		levelMin

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		levelMax

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		tagPrefix

    Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

Lumberjack.lvlib:LumberjackConfigDTOFromNative.vi

 error in (no error)

error in can accept error information wired from VIs previously called. Use this information to decide if any functionality should be bypassed in the event of errors from other VIs.

Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		status

    status is TRUE (X) if an error occurred or FALSE (checkmark) to indicate a warning or that no error occurred.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		code

    code is the error or warning code.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		source

    source describes the origin of the error or warning.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

LumberjackConfig

Top-level configuration: the Initialize inputs and the JSON file boundary (SRS-LMBR-050). Carries global settings plus the single default file appender; additional appenders are registered in code, not listed here. Field names match the JSON keys so native Unflatten From JSON maps directly, with the baseline (this cluster built from launch inputs) supplied as the default value so absent keys fall back per-key (SRS-LMBR-044-051).

    		schemaVersion

    JSON schema version; lets the validator reject configs it doesn't understand (SDD §4.2).

    		globalThreshold

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		defaultFileAppender

    Configuration for a file appender: an AppenderConfig nested as `common` plus file-specific fields. Field names match the JSON keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly (SRS-LMBR-030, 032-040). `delimiter` is fed into the CSVLayout the appender builds, not a separate setting (SDD 5.4).

      		common

      Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig). Carries identity, the per-appender authoritative threshold and selection filter (stage-2), backpressure settings, and the layout strategy. Field names match the JSON `common` keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly; `layout` is a Layout object set in code, not via JSON.

        		id

        Unique appender ID; used by the manager registry and unregister.

        		threshold

        Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

        thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

        statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

        offset math required).

        Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

        DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

        Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

        is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

        		filter

        Per-appender selection filter, applied after the appender threshold (SRS-LMBR-026, 027). In mirror mode, accept every statement at or above the appender threshold. In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

          		mode

          Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

          accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

          Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

          threshold.

          Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

          range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

          		levelMin

          Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

          thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

          statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

          offset math required).

          Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

          DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

          Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

          is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

          		levelMax

          Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

          thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

          statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

          offset math required).

          Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

          DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

          Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

          is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

          		tagPrefix

          Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

        		queueBound

        Maximum intake queue depth; 0 means unbounded (SRS-LMBR-055, 056).

        		dropPolicy

        Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

        full. Applies only when the appender's queue bound is greater than 0;

        an unbounded queue never drops. Discards are surfaced as a synthetic

        "N statements dropped" record, so loss is observable.

        DropOldest (default): discard the oldest queued statement to admit the

        new one. Favors recency.

        DropNewest: reject the incoming statement, keep what is already queued.

        LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

        statements first.

        		useUTC

        When TRUE, timestamps are formatted in UTC; when FALSE, in the local time zone. Per-appender and stamped onto the layout at Init, so different appenders may use different time frames (SRS-LMBR-013).

      		file

      Base folder for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

        		rootFolder

        Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

        		maxFileSize

        Rollover threshold in bytes; a write that would exceed it opens a new file (SRS-LMBR-033).

        		maxFileCount

        Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

        		baseName

        Provides a leading name to files for sorting Cannot include "_" in the base name.

        		extension

        File extension without the dot (e.g. "csv").

        		delimiter

        Column separator passed to the CSVLayout (e.g. "," or a tab).

        		calendarFolderTree

        When TRUE, place files in a dated sub-folder hierarchy under the root (SRS-LMBR-036).

    		source

    Right-click the error out indicator on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

Merge overlays JSON onto a baseline of this type; Resolve maps the validated result to the native LumberjackConfig.

        Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

        		maxFileSize

        Rollover threshold in bytes; a write that would exceed it opens a new file (SRS-LMBR-033).

        		maxFileCount

        Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

        		baseName

        Leading name applied to each file for sorting. Cannot contain an underscore, which is reserved as the timestamp separator in generated file names.

        		extension

        File extension without the dot (e.g. "csv").

        		delimiter

        Column separator passed to the CSVLayout (e.g. "," or a tab).

        		calendarFolderTree

        When TRUE, place files in a dated sub-folder hierarchy under the root (SRS-LMBR-036).

DropPolicyString

Context

DropPolicy

Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

full. Applies only when the appender's queue bound is greater than 0;

an unbounded queue never drops. Discards are surfaced as a synthetic

"N statements dropped" record, so loss is observable.

DropOldest (default): discard the oldest queued statement to admit the

new one. Favors recency.

DropNewest: reject the incoming statement, keep what is already queued.

LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

statements first.

error out

error out passes error or warning information out of a VI to be used by other VIs.

Right-click the error out indicator on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		status

    Right-click the error out indicator on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		code

    code is the error or warning code.

    Right-click the error out indicator on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		source

    source string describes the origin of the error or warning.

    Right-click the error out indicator on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

SeverityString

Context

Severity

Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

offset math required).

Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

Lumberjack.lvlib:IsFileNameSafe.vi

Pure filename-component predicate. Returns Safe? = FALSE with a Reason when the candidate contains a filesystem-illegal character (< > : " / \ | ? *) or a control character; empty is safe (the valid none sentinel for baseName and extension). Dots are legal. Does not raise an error itself; callers (Validate, CreateFileAppender) turn FALSE into config error 5020 with field context. No I/O.

Is a baseName/extension free of filesystem-illegal characters? (empty = safe)

Lumberjack.lvlib:ISO8601FileName.vi

Pure filename builder. Compose a log file name as an optional BaseName, an ISO

8601 timestamp, and the extension, e.g. Pump_2026-07-06T143005.csv, or 2026-07-06T143005.csv when BaseName is empty (SRS-LMBR-035). UseUTC selects the frame (UTC vs local); colons in the time are removed for Windows and the text sorts lexically in chronological order. Extension is normalized: a leading dot is optional, so "csv" and ".csv" both yield one dot, and an empty extension yields no trailing dot. Trusts inputs are valid (baseName is checked in Validate). Deterministic given inputs; no I/O.

Lumberjack.lvlib:PruneSelection.vi

Pure retention selection. Group the existing files by base name, then within each group keep the newest MaxFileCount (ordered by embedded ISO 8601 timestamp) and return the rest for deletion. Prunes only when MaxFileCount is positive; any non-positive value (including the -1 unbounded sentinel) keeps all and returns none (SRS-LMBR-034). Selects only; deletion happens in FileAppender:Prune. Deterministic; no I/O.

Per-base-name: keep newest MaxFileCount (>0); non-positive keeps all.

 ExistingFiles

    		RootFolder

maxFileCount

Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

Lumberjack.lvlib:RoutedFilterMatch.vi

Pure predicate for the routed filter test, evaluating only the Filter control (level band and tag prefix) and assuming the statement has already cleared the appender threshold. accepted is TRUE iff the statement's level is within the inclusive rank band [levelMin, levelMax] AND the sourceTag matches tagPrefix: an empty prefix matches any; a non-empty prefix matches on a dot-hierarchy boundary (app.db matches app.db and app.db.query, not app.database). Does not test the threshold and does not fault. Community.

 error in (no error)

error in can accept error information wired from VIs previously called. Use this information to decide if any functionality should be bypassed in the event of errors from other VIs.

Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		status

    status is TRUE (X) if an error occurred or FALSE (checkmark) to indicate a warning or that no error occurred.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		code

    code is the error or warning code.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

    		source

    source describes the origin of the error or warning.

    Right-click the error in control on the front panel and select Explain Error or Explain Warning from the shortcut menu for more information about the error.

Statement

One log record: a single logged event. Field order matches the fixed CSV

column order (SRS-LMBR-010, 012; SDD 5.4), so a layout reads fields in place.

`level` reuses the Severity typedef, keeping the rank encoding single-sourced.

`source tag` (logical, hierarchical) is kept distinct from `origin VI`

(physical emitting VI). `message` is the only caller-supplied field; the rest

are generated at log time.

    		timestamp

    When the event occurred; rendered as ISO 8601 when formatted (SRS-LMBR-011).

    		level

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		sourceTag

    Logical dot-separated hierarchical category (e.g. app.comms.tcp); defaults to the origin VI base name when unset (SRS-LMBR-013, 017).

    		originVI

    Physical name of the emitting VI, from the call chain; kept distinct from source tag.

    		message

    The caller-supplied text; the only field provided directly.

Filter

Per-appender selection filter, applied after the appender threshold (SRS-LMBR-026, 027). In mirror mode, accept every statement at or above the appender threshold. In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

    		mode

    Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

    accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

    Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

    threshold.

    Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

    range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

    		levelMin

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		levelMax

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		tagPrefix

    Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

Lumberjack.lvlib:ResolveHostRoot.vi

Resolve the host root that empty or relative log paths are computed against (SRS-LMBR-064). If HostApplicationPath is supplied, use it. Otherwise, when running as a built application (Application.Kind = Run Time System), return error 5000 (host application path required), since defaulting to the executable folder is often read-only under UAC; when running in the development system, fall back to Application Directory. Never derives a path from a Lumberjack VI's own location (no Current VI's Path), so paths stay correct inside a .lvlibp

Lumberjack.lvlib:RankCompare.vi

Pure severity comparison for threshold gating. Returns TRUE when Level passes Threshold, i.e. rank(Level) <= rank(Threshold), using the Severity enum ordinal as the rank (SRS-LMBR-005, 006). Used on the hot path by Log (stage-1) and by HandleStatement (stage-2). No state, no I/O; deterministic and unit-testable.

 Level

Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

offset math required).

Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

Lumberjack.lvlib:Sanitize.vi

Pure tag sanitization. Convert a raw string into a single valid hierarchy node by replacing every space and dot with an underscore, so a VI-derived name does not read as a false dot-separated hierarchy (SRS-LMBR-013). Trims leading and trailing whitespace first. No state, no I/O; deterministic.

Lumberjack.lvlib:AppenderConfig.ctl

 AppenderConfig

Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig). Carries identity, the per-appender authoritative threshold and selection filter (stage-2), backpressure settings, and the layout strategy. Field names match the JSON `common` keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly; `layout` is a Layout object set in code, not via JSON.

    		id

    Unique appender ID; used by the manager registry and unregister.

    		threshold

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		filter

    Per-appender selection filter, applied after the appender threshold (SRS-LMBR-026, 027). In mirror mode, accept every statement at or above the appender threshold. In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

      		mode

      Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

      accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

      Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

      threshold.

      Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

      range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

      		levelMin

      Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

      thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

      statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

      offset math required).

      Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

      DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

      Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

      is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

      		levelMax

      Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

      thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

      statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

      offset math required).

      Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

      DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

      Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

      is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

      		tagPrefix

      Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

    		queueBound

    Maximum intake queue depth; 0 means unbounded (SRS-LMBR-055, 056).

    		dropPolicy

    Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

    full. Applies only when the appender's queue bound is greater than 0;

    an unbounded queue never drops. Discards are surfaced as a synthetic

    "N statements dropped" record, so loss is observable.

    DropOldest (default): discard the oldest queued statement to admit the

    new one. Favors recency.

    DropNewest: reject the incoming statement, keep what is already queued.

    LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

    statements first.

    		useUTC

    When TRUE, timestamps are formatted in UTC; when FALSE, in the local time zone. Per-appender and stamped onto the layout at Init, so different appenders may use different time frames (SRS-LMBR-013).

Lumberjack.lvlib:DropPolicy.ctl

 DropPolicy

Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

full. Applies only when the appender's queue bound is greater than 0;

an unbounded queue never drops. Discards are surfaced as a synthetic

"N statements dropped" record, so loss is observable.

DropOldest (default): discard the oldest queued statement to admit the

new one. Favors recency.

DropNewest: reject the incoming statement, keep what is already queued.

LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

statements first.

Lumberjack.lvlib:FileAppenderConfig.ctl

 FileAppenderConfig

Configuration for a file appender: an AppenderConfig nested as `common` plus file-specific fields. Field names match the JSON keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly (SRS-LMBR-030, 032-040). `delimiter` is fed into the CSVLayout the appender builds, not a separate setting (SDD 5.4).

    		common

    Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig). Carries identity, the per-appender authoritative threshold and selection filter (stage-2), backpressure settings, and the layout strategy. Field names match the JSON `common` keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly; `layout` is a Layout object set in code, not via JSON.

      		id

      Unique appender id, matching the appender's common config id.

      		threshold

      thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

      statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

        Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

        		tagPrefix

        Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

      		queueBound

      Maximum intake queue depth; 0 means unbounded (SRS-LMBR-055, 056).

      		dropPolicy

      Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

      full. Applies only when the appender's queue bound is greater than 0;

      an unbounded queue never drops. Discards are surfaced as a synthetic

      "N statements dropped" record, so loss is observable.

      DropOldest (default): discard the oldest queued statement to admit the

      new one. Favors recency.

      DropNewest: reject the incoming statement, keep what is already queued.

      LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

      statements first.

      		useUTC

      When TRUE, timestamps are formatted in UTC; when FALSE, in the local time zone. Per-appender and stamped onto the layout at Init, so different appenders may use different time frames (SRS-LMBR-013).

    		file

      		rootFolder

      Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

      		maxFileSize

      Rollover threshold in bytes; a write that would exceed it opens a new file (SRS-LMBR-033).

      		maxFileCount

      Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

      		baseName

      Leading name applied to each file for sorting. Cannot contain an underscore, which is reserved as the timestamp separator in generated file names.

      		extension

      File extension without the dot (e.g. "csv").

      		delimiter

      Column separator passed to the CSVLayout (e.g. "," or a tab).

      		calendarFolderTree

      When TRUE, place files in a dated sub-folder hierarchy under the root (SRS-LMBR-036).

Lumberjack.lvlib:FileConfig.ctl

 FileConfig

    		rootFolder

    Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

    		maxFileSize

    Rollover threshold in bytes; a write that would exceed it opens a new file (SRS-LMBR-033).

    		maxFileCount

    Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

    		baseName

    Leading name applied to each file for sorting. Cannot contain an underscore, which is reserved as the timestamp separator in generated file names.

    		extension

    File extension without the dot (e.g. "csv").

    		delimiter

    Column separator passed to the CSVLayout (e.g. "," or a tab).

    		calendarFolderTree

    When TRUE, place files in a dated sub-folder hierarchy under the root (SRS-LMBR-036).

Lumberjack.lvlib:Filter.ctl

 Filter

Per-appender selection filter, applied after the appender threshold (SRS-LMBR-026, 027). In mirror mode, accept every statement at or above the appender threshold. In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

    		mode

    Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

    accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

    Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

    threshold.

    Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

    range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

    		levelMin

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		levelMax

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		tagPrefix

    Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

Lumberjack.lvlib:FilterMode.ctl

 FilterMode

Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

threshold.

Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

Lumberjack.lvlib:LumberjackConfig.ctl

 LumberjackConfig

Top-level configuration: the Initialize inputs and the JSON file boundary (SRS-LMBR-050). Carries global settings plus the single default file appender; additional appenders are registered in code, not listed here. Field names match the JSON keys so native Unflatten From JSON maps directly, with the baseline (this cluster built from launch inputs) supplied as the default value so absent keys fall back per-key (SRS-LMBR-044-051).

    		schemaVersion

    JSON schema version; lets the validator reject configs it doesn't understand (SDD §4.2).

    		globalThreshold

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		defaultFileAppender

    Configuration for a file appender: an AppenderConfig nested as `common` plus file-specific fields. Field names match the JSON keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly (SRS-LMBR-030, 032-040). `delimiter` is fed into the CSVLayout the appender builds, not a separate setting (SDD 5.4).

      		common

      Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig). Carries identity, the per-appender authoritative threshold and selection filter (stage-2), backpressure settings, and the layout strategy. Field names match the JSON `common` keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly; `layout` is a Layout object set in code, not via JSON.

        		id

        Unique appender id, matching the appender's common config id.

        		threshold

        Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

        thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

        statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

        offset math required).

        Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

        DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

          		tagPrefix

        		queueBound

Lumberjack.lvlib:RegistryEntry.ctl

 RegistryEntry

One entry in the LogManager's appender registry: an appender's id paired with its enqueuer. The manager uses id to find and address an appender (configure, unregister) and publishes the enqueuers as the Snapshot fan-out array (SDD 2.3).

    		id

    Unique appender id, matching the appender's common config id.

    		enqueuer

    The appender actor's enqueuer; target for control messages and a member of the Snapshot fan-out array.

Lumberjack.lvlib:RelayAppenderConfig.ctl

 RelayAppenderConfig

Configuration for a relay appender: an AppenderConfig nested as `common` plus a delivery mode and, for message mode, a consumer enqueuer (SRS-LMBR-023-025). In queue mode the enqueuer is unused and the relay exposes a queue refnum instead (SDD 5.6).

    		common

    Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig). Carries identity, the per-appender authoritative threshold and selection filter (stage-2), backpressure settings, and the layout strategy. Field names match the JSON `common` keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly; `layout` is a Layout object set in code, not via JSON.

      		id

      Unique appender ID; used by the manager registry and unregister.

      		threshold

      Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

      thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

      statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

      offset math required).

      Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

      DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

      is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

      		filter

        threshold.

        Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

        range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

        		levelMin

        Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

        thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

        statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

        offset math required).

        Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

        DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

        Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

        is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

        		levelMax

        Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

        thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

        statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

        offset math required).

        Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

        DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

        is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

        		tagPrefix

        Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

      		queueBound

      Maximum intake queue depth; 0 means unbounded (SRS-LMBR-055, 056).

      		dropPolicy

      Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

      LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

      statements first.

      		useUTC

      When TRUE, timestamps are formatted in UTC; when FALSE, in the local time zone. Per-appender and stamped onto the layout at Init, so different appenders may use different time frames (SRS-LMBR-013).

    		relayMode

    Selects how a relay appender delivers accepted statements to the

    application.

    Message (default): send each statement to a consumer enqueuer as a

    Log Statement Msg. Preferred for Actor Framework consumers.

    Queue: expose a queue refnum the application dequeues or flushes.

    Provided for non-actor consumers and Logger-style compatibility.

Lumberjack.lvlib:RelayMode.ctl

 RelayMode

Selects how a relay appender delivers accepted statements to the

application.

Message (default): send each statement to a consumer enqueuer as a

Log Statement Msg. Preferred for Actor Framework consumers.

Queue: expose a queue refnum the application dequeues or flushes.

Provided for non-actor consumers and Logger-style compatibility.

Lumberjack.lvlib:Severity.ctl

 Severity

Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

offset math required).

Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

Lumberjack.lvlib:Snapshot.ctl

 Snapshot

The Notifier payload the LogManager broadcasts to callers (SDD 2.1, 2.3). Read by every caller on the log hot path: globalThreshold gates stage-1, and the enqueuer array is the fan-out target list. The LogManager is the sole poster; callers only read (via Get Notifier Status), so reads are concurrent and non-destructive. Internal type, not part of the public API.

    		globalThreshold

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		appenderEnqueuers

    The current broadcast targets, one Enqueuer per registered appender. The LogManager posts a new array on register/unregister (SRS-LMBR-020, 028).

      		consumerEnqueuer

      <strong>Caller Enqueuer</strong> returns the reference the actor needs to send messages to its caller.

Lumberjack.lvlib:Statement.ctl

 Statement

One log record: a single logged event. Field order matches the fixed CSV

column order (SRS-LMBR-010, 012; SDD 5.4), so a layout reads fields in place.

`level` reuses the Severity typedef, keeping the rank encoding single-sourced.

`source tag` (logical, hierarchical) is kept distinct from `origin VI`

(physical emitting VI). `message` is the only caller-supplied field; the rest

are generated at log time.

    		timestamp

    When the event occurred; rendered as ISO 8601 when formatted (SRS-LMBR-011).

    		level

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		sourceTag

    Logical dot-separated hierarchical category (e.g. app.comms.tcp); defaults to the origin VI base name when unset (SRS-LMBR-013, 017).

    		originVI

    Physical name of the emitting VI, from the call chain; kept distinct from source tag.

    		message

    The caller-supplied text; the only field provided directly.

Lumberjack.lvlib:AppenderConfigDTO.ctl

String DTO mirror of the common AppenderConfig (SDD 4.2). threshold and dropPolicy are member-name strings; filter is a FilterDTO; id and queueBound are unchanged. Carries no Layout (config is data; the appender builds its Layout at InitCommon). Resolve maps this to the native AppenderConfig.

Lumberjack.lvlib:FileConfigDTO.ctl

 FileConfigDTO

    		rootFolder

    Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

    		maxFileSize

    Rollover threshold in bytes; a write that would exceed it opens a new file (SRS-LMBR-033).

    		maxFileCount

    Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

    		baseName

    Leading name applied to each file for sorting. Cannot contain an underscore, which is reserved as the timestamp separator in generated file names.

    		extension

    File extension without the dot (e.g. "csv").

    		delimiter

    Column separator passed to the CSVLayout (e.g. "," or a tab).

    		calendarFolderTree

    When TRUE, place files in a dated sub-folder hierarchy under the root (SRS-LMBR-036).

Lumberjack.lvlib:FilterDTO.ctl

String DTO mirror of Filter, used only as the Unflatten From JSON target and merge currency (SDD 4.2). mode is a FilterMode member name; levelMin/levelMax are Severity member names; tagPrefix is unchanged. Resolve maps this to the native Filter (names to enums). Not part of the public API.

 FilterDTO

String DTO mirror of Filter, used only as the Unflatten From JSON target and merge currency (SDD 4.2). mode is a FilterMode member name; levelMin/levelMax are Severity member names; tagPrefix is unchanged. Resolve maps this to the native Filter (names to enums). Not part of the public API.

    		mode

    Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

    accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

    Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

    threshold.

    Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

    range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

    		levelMin

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		levelMax

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		tagPrefix

    Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

Lumberjack.lvlib:LumberjackConfigDTO.ctl

 LumberjackConfigDTO

Top-level string DTO mirror of LumberjackConfig and the Unflatten From JSON target for the whole config file (SDD 4.2). globalThreshold is a Severity member name; defaultFileAppender is a FileAppenderConfigDTO; schemaVersion is unchanged. Merge overlays JSON onto a baseline of this type; Resolve maps the validated result to the native LumberjackConfig.

    		schemaVersion

    JSON schema version; lets the validator reject configs it doesn't understand (SDD §4.2).

    		globalThreshold

    Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for

    thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a

    statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

    offset math required).

    Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

    DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

    Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

    is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

    		defaultFileAppender

    Configuration for a file appender: an AppenderConfig nested as `common` plus file-specific fields. Field names match the JSON keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly (SRS-LMBR-030, 032-040). `delimiter` is fed into the CSVLayout the appender builds, not a separate setting (SDD 5.4).

      		common

      Common configuration shared by every appender (SRS-LMBR-029), nested as `common` inside each type-specific config (FileAppenderConfig, RelayAppenderConfig). Carries identity, the per-appender authoritative threshold and selection filter (stage-2), backpressure settings, and the layout strategy. Field names match the JSON `common` keys so Unflatten From JSON maps directly; `layout` is a Layout object set in code, not via JSON.

        		id

        Unique appender id, matching the appender's common config id.

        		threshold

        String representation of severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no

        offset math required).

        Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4),

        DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

        Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold

        is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

        		filter

        Per-appender selection filter, applied after the appender threshold (SRS-LMBR-026, 027). In mirror mode, accept every statement at or above the appender threshold. In routed mode, accept only statements whose rank falls in [level min, level max] and whose source tag matches `tag prefix` by hierarchical prefix (an empty prefix matches any). `mode` reuses FilterMode; the two level bounds reuse Severity, keeping rank encoding single-sourced.

          		mode

          Selects how an appender's selection filter decides which statements to

          accept, after the appender threshold has been applied.

          Mirror (default): accept every statement at or above the appender

          threshold.

          Routed: accept only statements matching the filter criteria, a level

          range and/or a hierarchical source-tag prefix.

          		levelMin

          Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

          Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

          Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

          		levelMax

          Severity level of a log statement, and the unit of comparison for thresholds. The numeric value of each item equals its rank, so a statement is delivered when its rank <= the active threshold (no offset math required).

          Levels emitted by the log VIs: FATAL(1), ERROR(2), WARN(3), INFO(4), DEBUG(5), TRACE(6). Lower rank = higher severity.

          Threshold-only sentinels (never emitted, used only where a threshold is set): OFF(0) disables all logging; ALL(7) passes every level.

          		tagPrefix

          Routed hierarchical prefix, dot-separated (e.g. app.db). Matches a tag equal to it or beginning with it plus a dot separator; empty matches any (SRS-LMBR-027).

        		queueBound

        Maximum intake queue depth; 0 means unbounded (SRS-LMBR-055, 056).

        		dropPolicy

        Selects which statement is discarded when a bounded appender queue is

        full. Applies only when the appender's queue bound is greater than 0;

        an unbounded queue never drops. Discards are surfaced as a synthetic

        "N statements dropped" record, so loss is observable.

        DropOldest (default): discard the oldest queued statement to admit the

        new one. Favors recency.

        DropNewest: reject the incoming statement, keep what is already queued.

        LevelAware: never discard ERROR or FATAL; shed lower-severity

        statements first.

        		useUTC

        When TRUE, timestamps are formatted in UTC; when FALSE, in the local time zone. Per-appender and stamped onto the layout at Init, so different appenders may use different time frames (SRS-LMBR-013).

      		fileConfig

      Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

        		rootFolder

        Base folder path for log files; empty means resolve from host application context (SRS-LMBR-039, 064).

        		maxFileSize

        Rollover threshold in bytes; a write that would exceed it opens a new file (SRS-LMBR-033).

        		maxFileCount

        Retention limit; oldest files beyond it are pruned; 0 keeps all (SRS-LMBR-034).

        		baseName

        Leading name applied to each file for sorting. Cannot contain an underscore, which is reserved as the timestamp separator in generated file names.

        		extension

        File extension without the dot (e.g. "csv").

        		delimiter

        Column separator passed to the CSVLayout (e.g. "," or a tab).

        		calendarFolderTree

        When TRUE, place files in a dated sub-folder hierarchy under the root (SRS-LMBR-036).
